	Select NFDados
	Skip
	nQtd = nQtd+1
Enddo

Select XMLTags

*** Monta NFe em arquivo XML

Delete File &lcArq
=Strtofile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcLinha), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<NFe xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcLinha), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<infNFe Id="NFe]+cId+[" versao="]+Thisform.versaol+[">]+ lcLinha), lcArq, .T.)
&&=Strtofile(Alltrim([<infNFe Id="NFe]+cId+[" versao="2.00" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)

Select XMLTags
Set Order To
Go Top

Do While Not Eof()
	cReg = c1
	nReg = Recno()

	If Inlist(Substr(c1, 7, 1), "B", "C", "E", "F", "G", "Q", "S", "O", "X", "U")
		Select * From XMLTags Where c1 = cReg Order By c1, c3 Into Cursor aux
		Go Top
		Scan
			=Strtofile(Alltrim(aux.c2) + lcLinha, lcArq, .T.)
		Endscan
		Select XMLTags
		Go nReg
		Do While c1=cReg
			Skip
		Enddo
	Else
		=Strtofile(Alltrim(XMLTags.c2) + lcLinha, lcArq, .T.)
		Select XMLTags
		Skip
	Endif
Enddo

*** Finaliza arquivo XML
=Strtofile([</infNFe>]+ lcLinha, lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</NFe>]+ lcLinha, lcArq, .T.)

**** Inclui inf Adicional    ****
lcInf1 = Filetostr(lcArq)
nIni=Atc('<infCpl>', lcInf1, 1)
nFim=Atc('</infCpl>', lcInf1, 1)
If nFim <> 0
	lcInf1 = Substr(lcInf1, 1, nIni+7) + lcInf + Substr(lcInf1, nFim)
	=Strtofile(lcInf1, lcArq, .F.)
Endif
**********************************



Return lcArq


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE esperaarq
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE esperaarq
parameters cArq, nTime, cMsg
*** nTime = qtde de segundos a esperar
LOCAL i, nT, j, msg

nT = nTime
i=0
j=0
DO WHILE NOT FILE(cArq) AND j < nT
	msg = IIF(VARTYPE(cMsg)<>'C',IIF(VAL(lcSer) < 900, 'Aguardando retorno da SEFAZ', 'Aguardando retorno do SCAN'), cMsg)
	WAIT window msg timeout 1
	j=j+1
ENDDO
If NOT FILE(cArq)
	Return .F.
ENDIF	
Return .T.


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE esperauniler
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE esperauniler
parameters cArq, nTime
LOCAL i
nTime = nTime
i=0
DO WHILE FILE(cArq) AND i < nTime
	WAIT window '' timeout 1
	i=i+1
ENDDO
RETURN

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE abregen
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE abregen
parameters cCod, nCol, cCodp 
PRIVATE i, d, t, l, p

SELECT NFTags
SEEK cCod
do while ALLTRIM(NFTags.C1) = cCod and not EOF()
	IF NFTags.C30				&& tag filho?
	   FOR i=2 to nCol step 1
	   	d=[NFDados.C]+ALLTRIM(STR(i))
		t=[NFTags.C]+ALLTRIM(STR(i))
		l=[NFTags.C]+ALLTRIM(STR(i))+"a"
		p=[NFTags.C]+ALLTRIM(STR(i))+"b"
		IF not EMPTY(&d) OR INLIST(&l, 1, 2) && grava se existe conteúdo ou se campo obrigatorio (1=numerico, 2=alfa)
			SELECT XMLTags
			APPEND BLANK
			replace c1 WITH cCodp+SUBSTR(cCod, 1, 1)
			replace c2 WITH [<]+ALLTRIM(&t)+[>]+ IIF(!EMPTY(&d), ALLTRIM(&d), IIF(&l=1, "0.00", "")) + [</]+ALLTRIM(&t)+[>]
			replace c3 WITH &p
			select NFTags
		ENDIF
	   ENDFOR 	
	ELSE
		IF not EMPTY(NFTags.C2)
			SELECT XMLTags
			APPEND BLANK
			replace c1 WITH cCodp+SUBSTR(cCod, 1, 1)
			replace c2 WITH [<]+ALLTRIM(NFTags.C2)+[>]
			replace c3 WITH NFTags.C2b
			select NFTags
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	SKIP
ENDDO
RETURN

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE fechagen
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE fechagen
parameters cCod, cCodp 
*** fecha tags abertas
SELECT NFTags
SEEK cCod
do while ALLTRIM(NFTags.C1) = cCod and not NFTags.C30 and not EOF()
	IF not EMPTY(NFTags.C2)
			SELECT XMLTags
			APPEND BLANK
			replace c1 WITH cCodp+SUBSTR(cCod, 1, 1)
			replace c2 WITH [</]+ALLTRIM(NFTags.C2)+[>]
			replace c3 WITH NFTags.C2c
			select NFTags
	ENDIF
	SKIP
ENDDO
RETURN

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE criachave
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE criachave
private uf, da, mo, se, tnf, nnf, cnf, cnpf, lcCha, lcDig, temi

SELECT NFDados

SEEK "B"

uf = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c2)
da = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c8)
mo = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c5)
se = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c6)
tnf = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c11)
temi = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c14)
nnf = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c7)
lcTpImp = IIF(ALLTRIM(NFDados.c14) = '1', 'RETRATO', 'PAISAGEM')
**	cnf = transform(NewId('ChaveXml'),"@L 99999999")

SEEK "C02"
cnpj = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c2)
cCnpj = cnpj		&& alimenta variavel para contar pastas de envio
cDEmis= SUBSTR(da, 1, 4) + SUBSTR(da, 6, 2) +  + SUBSTR(da, 9, 2)
cnf = transform(VAL(nnf) + VAL(cDEmis),"@L 99999999")

lcCha = uf + SUBSTR(da, 3,2) + SUBSTR(da, 6, 2) + cnpj+mo+TRANSFORM(VAL(se), "@L, 999")+TRANSFORM(VAL(nnf), "@L, 999999999")+temi+cnf
lcDig = THISFORM.digitoverificador(lcCha)
lcCha = lcCha + lcDig

SEEK "E"
cEmail = ALLTRIM(NFDados.c6)

*** Grava campos calculados pois eles năo vęm no txt ***
SEEK "B"
replace c3 with cnf
replace c15 with lcDig	


RETURN lcCha

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE digitoverificador
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE digitoverificador
parameters _key

Local i As Integer
Local j As Integer
Local k As Integer
Local DV As Double

j = 5
DV = 0.00
For i = 1 To 43 Step 1
j = Iif(j = 2, 9, j - 1)
K = j * Val(Substr(_Key , i, 1))
DV = DV + K
Release K
EndFor

DV = Mod(DV, 11)
DV = Iif(Between(DV, 0, 1), 0, 11 - DV)
Return Alltrim(Str(DV))


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cannfe
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cannfe
PRIVATE cTo, cAssunto, cAnexo, cCorpo, cFrom, cCC, cServer, cSenha, nPorta
PRIVATE lOk, cCampo, cComando, lcTeste, lcStat
PRIVATE lcDest, lcXml, lcQuery, lcArqXML, lcArqPDF

Local lcArq, lcTAmb, lcProt

lcArq = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + cId+"-ped-can.XML"
lcProt = crNotas.prots
lcTAmb = Iif(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, '2', '1')

DELETE FILE &lcArq
=StrToFile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcChr), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<cancNFe versao="]+thisform.versaol+[" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<infCanc Id="ID]+Alltrim(cId)+[">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpAmb>]+Alltrim(lcTAmb)+[</tpAmb>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xServ>]+"CANCELAR"+[</xServ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<chNFe>]+cId+[</chNFe>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<nProt>]+Alltrim(lcProt)+[</nProt>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xJust>]+"Cliente cancelou a venda nao desejando mais levar o produto"+[</xJust>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</infCanc>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</cancNFe>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)

&&=Strtofile(Alltrim([<cancNFe xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" versao="2.00" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)

cCorpo = ALLTRIM(LocalEmp.textonfe)
cFrom  = ALLTRIM(LocalEmp.emailnfe)
cCC    = ALLTRIM(LocalEmp.emailnfe)
cServer= ALLTRIM(LocalEmp.servs)
cSenha = ALLTRIM(LocalEmp.senhas)
nPorta = LocalEmp.portas

lOk = .F.
cCampo=''

DO WHILE .T.
	lcXml = cId+"-ped-can.XML"
	**** delete arquivo de processo anterior (se houver)
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-can.XML"
	DELETE FILE &lcDest
	
	*** Enviar arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+lcXml
	=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Envia Cancelamento ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Verifica se retornou erro
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-can.err"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 3)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		exit
	EndIf

	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-can.XML"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 180)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		i=2
		lcStat = ''
		do while LEN(lcStat)=0 and i>0			&& procura ultima ocorrencia válida do cStat 
			lcStat = STREXTRACT(cLinha,"<cStat>","</cStat>",i)
			i=i-1
		ENDDO
		i=2
		lcMotivo = ''
		do while LEN(lcMotivo)=0 and i>0			&& procura ultima ocorrencia válida de xMotivo 
			lcMotivo = STREXTRACT(cLinha,"<xMotivo>","</xMotivo>",i)
			i=i-1
		ENDDO

		cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + lcMotivo
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Retorno do Cancelamento Ok. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
		lcArq = lcDest
		lOk = "101"$(lcStat) and "CANC"$(upper(cCampo)) 
		IF lOk
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Nota cancelada. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
			lcDest=lcPathNFe + lcPAutorizados + SUBSTR(cDEmis, 1, 6) + [01\] + cId + [-procCancNFe.xml]
			IF not (THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 10))
				lcDest=lcPathNFe + lcPAutorizados + cDEmis + [\] + cId + [-procCancNFe.xml]
				IF not (THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 10))
					COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest	&& se nao veio o distribuicao, pega o retorno
				ENDIF
			endif			
			replace stats with 'CAN' in crNotas
			replace statts with '0' in crNotas
			DELETE FILE &lcArq
		ELSE
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Nota năo cancelada. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
			DELETE FILE &lcArq
		endif
	else
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Cancelamento. Arquivo de retorno năo veio. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
		cCampo = "NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + 'Nao houve resposta da Sefaz. Tente mais tarde.'
	EndIf
	EXIT	
EndDo
	  
IF lOk	
	cTo = cEmail
	cAssunto = "Nota fiscal cancelada: " + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9)
	cAnexo = lcDest

	=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Nota cancelada-envio email. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	IF Messagebox([Confirma envio de e-mail para: ] + cTo + ["?"], 4+32, [Nota fiscal cancelada]) = 6
		IF enviaEmail(cTo, cCorpo, cAssunto, cAnexo, cFrom, cCC)
			WAIT window [Email enviado com sucesso]
		ENDIF
	ENDIF

	*** Faz bachup do xml
	lcArq = lcDest
	lcDest=lcBkp+cId+[-procCancNFe.xml]
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Le conteudo do xml para gravar no sigmvnfi***
	cConteudoxml = FILETOSTR(lcArq)

	=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Nota cancelada-XML. ]+lcChr+cConteudoxml, lcLog, .T.)
	**** atualiza a base com os arquivos gerados ****
	SELECT crSigmvNfi
	SCATTER memvar memo
	m.canxml = cConteudoxml 	&& conteudo do arquivo xml
	m.cancelas = .T.			&& seta nota cancelada
	GATHER memvar memo
	IF Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update([crSigMvNfi])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigMvNfi)])
	ELSE
		IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	*** le protocolo de cancelamento ***
	i=2
	cProt = ''
	do while LEN(cProt)=0 and i>0			&& procura ultima ocorrencia válida de xMotivo 
		cProt=STREXTRACT(cConteudoxml,"<nProt>","</nProt>",i)
		i=i-1
	ENDDO
ELSE
	**** verifica e mostra erros retornados
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-can.err"
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + alltrim(cLinha)
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Erro Retornado: ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
	EndIf
	Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da SEFAZ])

	**** grava erro retornado na area do PDF - Mena 06/03/2013 ****
	SELECT crSigmvNfi
	SCATTER memvar memo
	m.nfepdf = IIF(ISNULL(m.nfepdf),'', ALLTRIM(m.nfepdf))+'--->'+STRCONV(cCampo,11)
	GATHER memvar memo
	IF Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update([crSigMvNfi])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigMvNfi)])
	ELSE
		IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	**********************************************

ENDIF
	
RETURN lOk

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE consnfe
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE consnfe
PRIVATE cTo, cAssunto, cAnexo, cCorpo, cFrom, cCC, cServer, cSenha
PRIVATE lOk, lOkD, cCampo, cComando, lcTeste
PRIVATE lcDest, lcXml, lcAux, lcQuery, lcArqXML, lcArqPDF

Local lcArq, lcTAmb, lcProt

cId = IIF(EMPTY(ALLTRIM(LocalNFis.nfechv)), cId,ALLTRIM(LocalNFis.nfechv))	&& mena - 29/01/2015 - incluido para recuperar xml emitido pelo emissor
lcArq = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + cId+"-ped-sit.XML"
lcTAmb = Iif(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, '2', '1')

DELETE FILE &lcArq
=StrToFile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcChr), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<consSitNFe versao="]+thisform.versaol+[" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpAmb>]+lcTAmb+[</tpAmb>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xServ>]+"CONSULTAR"+[</xServ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<chNFe>]+cId+[</chNFe>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</consSitNFe>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)

&&=Strtofile(Alltrim([<consSitNFe xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" versao="2.00" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
lOk = .F.
lOkD = .F.
cCampo=''

DO WHILE .T.
	lcXml = cId+"-nfe.XML"
	**** Pede re envio de XML para nota já autorizada ****
	lcDest = lcPathNFe + lcPAutorizados + cDEmis + [\] + cId + [-procNFe.xml]
	IF !FILE(lcDest) and crNotas.stats = 'EMI'
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Nota já autorizada e XML inexite. ], lcLog, .T.)

		*** Valida arquivo atraves da UNINFe
		lcAux = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + cId+"-nfe.XML"
		lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPValidar+lcXml
		COPY file &lcAux to &lcDest

		** Verifica se arquivo validado ok
		lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPValidar+lcPValidado+lcXml
		=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 10, 'Aguardando validaçăo')
		IF FILE(lcDest)
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Arquivo validado. ]+lcdest, lcLog, .T.)
			lcAux = lcPathNFe + lcPEmProc + lcXml
			COPY FILE &lcDest to &lcAux
			DELETE FILE &lcDest
		ELSE
			cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + 'Problema ao assinar o arquivo. Verifique o certificado.'
			EXIT 
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	
	lcXml = cId+"-ped-sit.XML"
	**** delete arquivo de processo anterior (se houver)
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-sit.XML"
	DELETE FILE &lcDest

	*** Valida arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPValidar+lcXml
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	** Verifica se arquivo validado ok
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPValidar+lcPValidado+lcXml
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 10, 'Aguardando validaçăo')
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Arquivo validado. ]+lcdest, lcLog, .T.)
		lcAux = lcPathNFe + lcPEmProc + lcXml
		COPY FILE &lcDest to &lcAux
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
	ELSE
		cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + 'Problema ao assinar o arquivo. Verifique o certificado.'
		EXIT 
	ENDIF


	*** Enviar arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+lcXml
	=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Consulta Nfe. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Verifica se retornou erro
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-sit.err"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 3)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		exit
	ENDIF
	
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-sit.XML"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 180)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)

		cProt=STREXTRACT(cLinha,"<nProt>","</nProt>",1)

		i=2
		lcStat = ''
		do while LEN(lcStat)=0 and i>0			&& procura ultima ocorrencia válida do cStat 
			lcStat = STREXTRACT(cLinha,"<cStat>","</cStat>",i)
			i=i-1
		ENDDO
		i=2
		lcMotivo = ''
		do while LEN(lcMotivo)=0 and i>0			&& procura ultima ocorrencia válida de xMotivo 
			lcMotivo = STREXTRACT(cLinha,"<xMotivo>","</xMotivo>",i)
			i=i-1
		ENDDO

		cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + lcMotivo
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
		lOk = "100"$(lcStat) and "AUTORIZA"$(upper(cCampo)) 
		lOkD = "DENEGA"$(upper(cCampo)) 
		IF lOk		&& autorizada
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Retorno da Consulta Nfe Ok. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
			replace stats with 'EMI' in crNotas
			replace statts with '0' in crNotas
			replace prots with cProt in crNotas
		ELSE
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Retorno da Consulta Nfe năo Ok. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		endif
		IF lOkD		&& denegada
			=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Retorno da Consulta Nfe Ok. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
			replace stats with 'DEN' in crNotas
			replace statts with '0' in crNotas
			replace prots with cProt in crNotas
		endif
	ELSE
		cCampo = "NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + 'Nao houve resposta da Sefaz. Tente mais tarde.'
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Retorno da Consulta năo veio. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	EndIf
	EXIT	
EndDo

If !lOk and !lOKD
	**** verifica e mostra erros retornados
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+cId+"-sit.err"
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		cCampo="NF:" + SUBSTR(cId, 26, 9) + Chr(10) + alltrim(cLinha)
		=StrToFile(lcChr+space(4)+[-Erro retornado: ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
	EndIf
	Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da SEFAZ])
	**** grava erro retornado na area do PDF - Mena 06/03/2013 ****
	SELECT crSigmvNfi
	SCATTER memvar memo
	m.nfepdf = IIF(ISNULL(m.nfepdf),'', ALLTRIM(m.nfepdf))+'--->'+STRCONV(cCampo,11)
	GATHER memvar memo
	IF Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update([crSigMvNfi])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigMvNfi)])
	ELSE
		IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	**********************************************
ENDIF
	
RETURN lOk

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE inunfe
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE inunfe
parameters pSerie, pNFi, pNFf
PRIVATE lOk, cCampo, cComando, lcTeste
PRIVATE lcDest, lcXml, lcQuery, lcArqXML, lcArqPDF

Local lcArq, lcTAmb, lcProt, lcBkp, lcData
Local lcNIni, lcNFim
Local lcUf, lcAno, lcTeste

lcUf  = ALLTRIM(str(ThisForm.CodIBGEUF(LocalEmp.estas)))
lcData = DTOS(DATE())
lcAno = SUBSTR(DTOS(DATE()),3,2)
lcEmp = LocalEmp.Cemps

lcNIni = TRANSFORM(VAL(ALLTRIM(thisform.cntOperacoes.getInuIni.value)), "@L 999999999")	&& formato para nome do arquivo 
lcNFim = TRANSFORM(VAL(ALLTRIM(thisform.cntOperacoes.getInuFim.value)), "@L 999999999")	&& formato para nome do arquivo
lcTAmb = IIF(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, '2', '1')

If Type([pNFi])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pNFi)
		lcNIni = Alltrim(pNFi)
	EndIf 
EndIf 

If Type([pNFf])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pNFf)
		lcNFim = Alltrim(pNFf)
	EndIf 
EndIf 

If Type([pSerie])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pSerie)
		lcSer = Padr(pSerie, 3)
	EndIf 
EndIf 	

lcId = lcUf+lcAno+lcCnpj+'55'+lcSer+lcNIni+lcNFim
lcArq = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + lcId+"-ped-inu.XML"

lcNIni = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(lcNIni), "@R 999999999"))	&& formato para campo dentro do arquivo 
lcNFim = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(lcNFim), "@R 999999999"))	&& formato para campo dentro do arquivo
lcSer  = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(lcSer), "@R 999"))			&& formato para campo dentro do arquivo
lOk    = .T.
lcBkp = lcPBkp+lcCnpj+[\]+SUBSTR(DTOS(DATE()), 1, 6)+[\]	&& seta pasta de buckup
Try 
	IF not DIRECTORY(lcBkp)
		MKDIR &lcBkp
	endif	
Catch
	MessageBox([Erro na criaçăo da pasta ] + lcBkp,0+48,[Aviso])
	lOk    = .F.
EndTry 

If !lOk 
	Return .F.
EndIf 

DELETE FILE &lcArq
=StrToFile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcChr), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<inutNFe versao="]+thisform.versaol+[" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">] + lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<infInut Id="ID]+lcId+[">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpAmb>]+lcTAmb+[</tpAmb>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xServ>]+"INUTILIZAR"+[</xServ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<cUF>]+lcuf+[</cUF>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<ano>]+lcano+[</ano>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<CNPJ>]+lccnpj+[</CNPJ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<mod>]+'55'+[</mod>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<serie>]+lcSer+[</serie>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<nNFIni>]+lcNIni+[</nNFIni>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<nNFFin>]+lcNFim+[</nNFFin>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xJust>]+'Ocorreu uma falha no sistema que pulou a sequencia de numeracao'+[</xJust>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</infInut>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</inutNFe>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)

&&=Strtofile(Alltrim([<inutNFe xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" versao="2.00" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">] + lcChr), lcArq, .T.)

lOk = .F.
cCampo=''

DO WHILE .T.

	lcXml = lcId+"-ped-inu.XML"
	**** delete arquivo de processo anterior (se houver)
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-inu.XML"
	DELETE FILE &lcDest
	
	*** Enviar arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+lcXml
	=StrToFile(lcChr+DTOS(DATE())+[-Inutiliza numeraçăo. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Verifica se retornou erro
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-inu.err"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 2)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		exit
	ENDIF
	
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-inu.XML"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 180)
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		pIni=ATC("<cStat>", cLinha, 1)	&& pega CODIGO DE RETORNO dentro do xml
		pFim=ATC("</cStat>", cLinha, 1)
		lcStat=SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+7, pFim-(pIni+7))
		pIni=ATC("<nProt>", cLinha, 1)	&& pega CODIGO DE RETORNO dentro do xml
		pFim=ATC("</nProt>", cLinha, 1)
		cProt=SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+7, pFim-(pIni+7))
		pIni=ATC("<xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		pFim=ATC("</xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		cCampo=SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+9, pFim-(pIni+9))
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-Inutiliza Retorno. ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
		lOk = "102"$(lcStat) 
		IF lOk
			&& gravar inutilizacao
			SELECT crNotas
			APPEND BLANK				&& cria linha especifica para inutilizacao
			replace emps with lcEmp in crNotas
			replace Oks with .T. in crNotas
			replace ids with lcId in crNotas
			replace prots with cProt in crNotas
			replace lotes with lcNIni in crNotas	&& numero inicial
			replace recibos with lcNFim in crNotas	&& numero final
			replace stats with 'INU' in crNotas
			replace dopes with 'INUTILIZACAO' in crNotas
			replace numes with VAL(lcNIni) in crNotas
			=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-Inutiliza Ok. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
		endif
	ELSE
		cCampo = lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-Inutiliza - Nao houve resposta da Sefaz. Tente mais tarde.]
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-Retorno de inutilizaçăo năo veio. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	EndIf
	EXIT	
EndDo

IF lOk	
	*** Faz bachup do xml
	lcArq = lcPathNFe + lcPAutorizados + lcData + [\] + lcId + [-procInutNFe.xml]
	lcDest=lcBkp+lcId+[-procInutNFe.xml]
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest
	Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da SEFAZ])
Else
	**** verifica e mostra erros retornados
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-inu.err"
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		cCampo=alltrim(cLinha)
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-Erro Retornado: ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
	EndIf
	Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da SEFAZ])
ENDIF

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE conserv
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE conserv
**** consulta situaçăo do serviço da sefaz ****

PRIVATE lOk, cCampo, cComando, lcTeste
PRIVATE lcDest, lcXml, lcQuery, lcArqXML, lcArqPDF

Local lcArq, lcTAmb, lcHoje, lcUf, lcId

lcHoje = TTOC(DATETIME())
lcId = SUBSTR(lcHoje,7, 4) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 4, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 1, 2) + [T] + ;
		SUBSTR(lcHoje, 12, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 15, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 18, 2)
lcArq = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + lcId +[-ped-sta.XML]

lcUf  = ALLTRIM(str(ThisForm.CodIBGEUF(LocalEmp.estas)))
lcTAmb = IIF(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, '2', '1')


**** Verifica status do serviço da SEFAZ ****

DELETE FILE &lcArq
=StrToFile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcChr), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<consStatServ versao="]+thisform.versaol+[" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpAmb>]+lcTAmb+[</tpAmb>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<cUF>]+lcUF+[</cUF>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpEmis>]+[1]+[</tpEmis>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)		&& consulta tpEmis= normal (Sefaz)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xServ>]+[STATUS]+[</xServ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</consStatServ>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)

&&=Strtofile(Alltrim([<consStatServ xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" versao="2.00" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)


lOk = .F.
cCampo=''

DO WHILE .T.

	lcXml = lcId+"-ped-sta.XML"
	**** delete arquivo de processo anterior (se houver)
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.XML"
	DELETE FILE &lcDest
	
	*** Enviar arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+lcXml
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Verifica se retornou erro
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.err"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 3, 'Aguardando retorno da SEFAZ')
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		exit
	ENDIF
	
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.XML"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 180, 'Aguardando retorno da SEFAZ')
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		pIni=ATC("<cStat>", cLinha, 1)	&& pega CODIGO DE RETORNO dentro do xml
		pFim=ATC("</cStat>", cLinha, 1)
		lcStat=SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+7, pFim-(pIni+7))
		pIni=ATC("<xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		pFim=ATC("</xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		cCampo="Consulta Situaçăo do Serviço" + Chr(10) + SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+9, pFim-(pIni+9))
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SEFAZ-Retorno da Consulta Situaçăo do Serviço. ]+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		lOk = "107"$(lcStat) 
	ELSE
		cCampo = 'Nao houve resposta da Sefaz. Tente mais tarde.'
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SEFAZ-Retorno Consulta situaçăo do serviço năo veio. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	EndIf
	EXIT	
EndDo

If !lOk
	**** verifica e mostra erros retornados
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.err"
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		cCampo=alltrim(cLinha)
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SEFAZ-Erro Retornado: ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
		**** grava erro retornado na area do PDF - Mena 06/03/2013 ****
		SELECT crSigmvNfi
		SCATTER memvar memo
		m.nfepdf = IIF(ISNULL(m.nfepdf),'', ALLTRIM(m.nfepdf))+'--->'+STRCONV(cCampo,11)
		GATHER memvar memo
		IF Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update([crSigMvNfi])
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigMvNfi)])
		ELSE
			IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
				=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
			ENDIF
		ENDIF
		**********************************************
	EndIf
ENDIF

Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da SEFAZ])

RETURN thisform.conscan()

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE conscan
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE conscan
parameters lpStat

********************************************
**** Verifica status do serviço da SCAN ****
********************************************

PRIVATE lOk, cCampo, cComando, lcTeste
PRIVATE lcDest, lcXml, lcQuery, lcArqXML, lcArqPDF

Local lcArq, lcTAmb, lcHoje, lcUf, lcId

lcUf  = ALLTRIM(str(ThisForm.CodIBGEUF(LocalEmp.estas)))
lcTAmb = IIF(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, '2', '1')

lcHoje = TTOC(DATETIME())
lcId = SUBSTR(lcHoje,7, 4) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 4, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 1, 2) + [T] + ;
		SUBSTR(lcHoje, 12, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 15, 2) + SUBSTR(lcHoje, 18, 2)
lcArq = cPathUni  + lcPTxt + lcId +[-ped-sta.XML]

DELETE FILE &lcArq
=StrToFile([], lcArq)

=Strtofile(Alltrim([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>]+ lcChr), lcArq,.T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<consStatServ versao="]+thisform.versaol+[" xmlns="http://www.portalfiscal.inf.br/nfe">]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpAmb>]+lcTAmb+[</tpAmb>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<cUF>]+lcUF+[</cUF>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<tpEmis>]+[3]+[</tpEmis>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)		&& consulta tpEmis= SCAN - nacional
=Strtofile(Alltrim([<xServ>]+[STATUS]+[</xServ>]+ lcChr), lcArq, .T.)
=Strtofile([</consStatServ>]+ lcChr, lcArq, .T.)


lOk = .F.
cCampo=''

DO WHILE .T.

	lcXml = lcId+"-ped-sta.XML"
	**** delete arquivo de processo anterior (se houver)
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.XML"
	DELETE FILE &lcDest
	
	*** Enviar arquivo atraves da UNINFe
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+lcXml
	COPY file &lcArq to &lcDest

	*** Verifica se retornou erro
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.err"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 3, 'Aguardando retorno do SCAN')
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		exit
	ENDIF
	
	lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.XML"
	=THISFORM.esperaarq(lcDest, 180, 'Aguardando retorno do SCAN')
	IF FILE(lcDest)
		cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
		pIni=ATC("<cStat>", cLinha, 1)	&& pega CODIGO DE RETORNO dentro do xml
		pFim=ATC("</cStat>", cLinha, 1)
		lcStat=SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+7, pFim-(pIni+7))
		pIni=ATC("<xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		pFim=ATC("</xMotivo>", cLinha, 1)
		cCampo="Consulta Situaçăo do Serviço" + Chr(10) + SUBSTR(cLinha,pIni+9, pFim-(pIni+9))
		DELETE FILE &lcDest
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SCAN-Retorno da Consulta Situaçăo do Serviço. ]+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
		lOk = "107"$(lcStat) 
	ELSE
		cCampo = 'SCAN-Nao houve resposta. Tente mais tarde.'
		=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SCAN-Retorno de Consulta situaçăo do serviço năo veio. ]+lcDest, lcLog, .T.)
	EndIf
	EXIT	
EndDo

**** verifica e mostra erros retornados
lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPRetorno+lcId+"-sta.err"
IF FILE(lcDest)
	cLinha = FILETOSTR(lcDest)
	cCampo=alltrim(cLinha)
	=StrToFile(lcChr+SPACE(4)+[-SCAN-Erro Retornado: ]+lcChr+cLinha, lcLog, .T.)
	DELETE FILE &lcDest
EndIf

IF VARTYPE(lpStat)<>'C'	&& se só consulta de status năo mostra mensagem 
	Messagebox(STRCONV(cCampo,11), 0+64, [Retorno da Receita Federal])
	**** grava erro retornado na area do PDF - Mena 06/03/2013 ****
	SELECT crSigmvNfi
	SCATTER memvar memo
	m.nfepdf = IIF(ISNULL(m.nfepdf),'', ALLTRIM(m.nfepdf))+'--->'+STRCONV(cCampo,11)
	GATHER memvar memo
	IF Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update([crSigMvNfi])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigMvNfi)])
	ELSE
		IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
	**********************************************
	
ENDIF

RETURN lOk

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE apptxt
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE apptxt
***********************************************************************************************
parameters lcTXT
LOCAL lcTexto, lclinha, lcCampo, i, j, lnTam

SET MEMOWIDTH TO 5000
lcTexto = FILETOSTR(lcTXT)

FOR j=1 to 10000 step 1
	lcLinha = MLINE(lcTexto, j) 
	IF EMPTY(lcLinha)
		exit
	ENDIF
	SELECT nfdados
	APPEND BLANK
	FOR i=1 to 24 step 1
		d=[NFDados.C]+ALLTRIM(STR(i))
		lnTam= AT('|', lcLinha, 1)
		IF lnTam = 0
			lcCampo = SUBSTR(lcLinha, 1)
		ELSE
			lcCampo = SUBSTR(lcLinha, 1, lntam-1)
			lcLinha = SUBSTR(lcLinha, lntam+1)
		ENDIF
		replace &d WITH lcCampo
		IF lnTam = 0
			exit
		endif	
	ENDFOR
ENDFOR

RETURN
***********************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE conectado
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE conectado
**** Verifica se a conexao com a internet está ativa ****
DECLARE LONG InternetGetConnectedState IN "wininet.dll" LONG, LONG
IF internetgetconnectedstate(0, 0) = 1
	RETURN .T.
ELSE
	RETURN .F.
ENDIF


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE inunfce
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE inunfce
parameters pSerie, pNFi, pNFf
LOCAL lcNF, lnRet, lcNIni, lcNFim, lcCod, lcDes

*** mena 05/08/2015 ***

DECLARE integer tCFInutilizar_NFCe_Daruma  in 'DarumaFramework' string StrnNFInic, string StrnNFFim, string StrNSerie, string StrJustificativa
DECLARE integer regRetornarValor_NFCe_Daruma in 'DarumaFramework' String StrTagNFCe, String StrValorTagNFCe
DECLARE integer rAvisoErro_NFCe_Daruma in 'DarumaFramework' String StrCodigo, String StrMensagem

lcNIni = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(ALLTRIM(thisform.cntOperacoes.getInuIni.value)), "@R 999999999"))
lcNFim = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(ALLTRIM(thisform.cntOperacoes.getInuFim.value)), "@R 999999999"))

If Type([pNFi])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pNFi)
		lcNIni = Alltrim(pNFi)
	EndIf 
EndIf 

If Type([pNFf])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pNFf)
		lcNFim = Alltrim(pNFf)
	EndIf 
EndIf 

*** Mena - 07/08/2018 - ajuste no numero de serie ***
lcSer = Padr(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getSeries.Value, 3)

If Type([pSerie])=[C]
	If Not IsEmpty(pSerie)
		lcSer = Padr(pSerie, 3)
	EndIf 
EndIf 	

lcD1 = IIF(ISDIGIT(SUBSTR(lcSer,1,1)),SUBSTR(lcSer,1,1),'')
lcD2 = IIF(ISDIGIT(SUBSTR(lcSer,2,1)),SUBSTR(lcSer,2,1),'')
lcD3 = IIF(ISDIGIT(SUBSTR(lcSer,3,1)),SUBSTR(lcSer,3,1),'')
lcSer = lcd1+lcd2+lcd3
&&lcSer  = ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(VAL(lcSer), "@R 999"))			&& formato para campo dentro do arquivo

*** pega informacoes da nota para guardar no sistema ***
lcNF= SPACE(6)
lnRet = regRetornarValor_NFCe_Daruma('IDE\nNF', @lcNf) 
=MostraErro(lnRet)	&& verifica se voltou erro e apresenta erro

IF VAL(lcNF) <= VAL(lcNFim)
	Messagebox([O intervalo abrange numeros que ainda podem ser usados], 0+64, [Inutilizaçăo Inválida])
	RETURN
ENDIF

WAIT [Aguarde. Preparando e Enviando Inutilizaçăo para SEFAZ!!] window NOWAIT

lnRet = tCFInutilizar_NFCe_Daruma(lcNIni, lcNFim, lcSer, 'Pulo na numeracao')
IF lnRet <> 0 and !MostraErro(lnRet)	&& verifica se voltou erro e apresenta erro
ENDIF

lcCod = SPACE(4)
lcDes = SPACE(600)
IF rAvisoErro_NFCe_Daruma(@lcCod, @lcDes)=1
	IF lnRet = 1 && se emitiu a nota, mostra a mensagem e continua
		WAIT ALLTRIM(lcDes) window NOWAIT
	ELSE
		MESSAGEBOX(ALLTRIM(lcDes), 0, 'Retorno NFCe')
	ENDIF
ENDIF

IF 'HOMOLOGA'$UPPER(lcDes)			&& se inutilizou grava registro 
	&& gravar inutilizacao
	WAIT clear 
	Messagebox([Inutilizaçăo executada com sucesso], 0+64, [INUTILIZACAO])
	SELECT crNotas
	APPEND BLANK				&& cria linha especifica para inutilizacao
	replace emps with lcEmp in crNotas
	replace Oks with .T. in crNotas
	replace lotes with lcNIni in crNotas	&& numero inicial
	replace recibos with lcNFim in crNotas	&& numero final
	replace stats with 'INU' in crNotas
	replace dopes with 'INUTILIZACAO NFCe' in crNotas
	replace numes with VAL(lcNIni) in crNotas
ENDIF

RETURN

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE leries

PROCEDURE leries
parameters pcEstasD

LOCAL lcIES, laIES
*** Mena - monta tabela de inscriçăo estadual do substituto tributário
lcIES = []

IF !INLIST(localEmp.cemps,[ECO],[SVP])
	RETURN lcIES
ENDIF

lcEstasD = Iif(Type([pcEstasD])=[C],pcEstasD,LocalCliD.estas)

IF !(LocalNFis.especienfs='CFNC' and localEmp.estas <> lcEstasD)	&& tem partilha
	RETURN lcIES
ENDIF

*** mena - 16/07/2017 - pega iest do cadastro interestadual ***
lcIES = localufd.iest

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE processamentoinutilizadas
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE processamentoinutilizadas
parameters pEmp, pSerie, pCnpj, pNFi, pNFf

*** Mena - 03/06/2019 - pega informacoes do Responsável tecnico
lcRTcnpj = Alltrim(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(LocalParac.cifcnpjs, [.], []), [-], []), [/], []))
lcRTcont = Alltrim(LocalParac.cifconts)
lcRTemai = Alltrim(LocalParac.cifendes)
lcRTtel  = Alltrim(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(LocalParac.ciftels, [(], []), [-], []), [)], []))

llOks = .T.
llNfe = .F.		&& indica que năo processou NFe
lnAca = Thisform.cntOperacoes.optAcao.Value
lnReg = Thisform.cntOperacoes.cmbRegime.ListIndex && 1-Simples Nacional, 2-Lucro Presumido, 3-Lucro Real, 4-Lucro Arbitrado
lnComSt = 0
lcChave = ''
lcFonte = ''
lcVerao = Iif(Thisform.cntOperacoes.chkHVerao.Value=1,'02:00','03:00')	&& seta formato da hora conforme horario de verăo ou năo
llFpf   = Thisform.cntOperacoes.chkVenc.Value=1							&& mena 20/10/2016 - mostra duplicatas com vencimento depois de hoje
llSub   = Thisform.cntOperacoes.OptSub.Value

* Comandos Para Montar Os Arquivos de Notas Fiscais
lnB_Amb = Iif(Thisform.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 2, 2, 1) && Identificaçăo do Ambiente (1 - Produçăo / 2 - Homologaçăo)
lcA_Ids = [NFe]
lnB_PrE = 0 			&& Processo de emissăo da NF-e
lcA_Ver = Thisform.Versaol		&& Mena - 05/06/2018 - pega versao do layout nos parametros
Do Case
Case (Thisform.cntOperacoes.optAmbiente.Value = 1)
	lcB_PrV = Thisform.Versao
Otherwise
	lcB_PrV = [TESTE ] + Thisform.Versao && Identificador da versăo do processo de emissăo (informar a versăo do aplicativo
Endcase

Zap In crSigPrNfe

If !(Inlist(lnAca, 1,2,3,5))
	If Thisform.GeraNfeInutilizadas(pEmp, pSerie, pCnpj, pNFi, pNFf)	&& entra no processamento da nfe quando inutilizaçăo/consulta serviço
		If Used([crNotas])
			If Inlist(lnAca,4,7) And Not Eof('crNotas')
				Insert Into crSigPrNfe (EmpDopNums, Emps, Dopes, Numes, DataS, Usuars, cidchaves, ids, lotes, recibos, prots, stats) ;
					Values (crNotas.Emps + crNotas.Dopes + Str(crNotas.Numes, 6), crNotas.Emps, crNotas.Dopes, crNotas.Numes, Datetime(), Usuar, fUniqueIds(), crNotas.ids, crNotas.lotes, crNotas.recibos, ;
					crNotas.prots, crNotas.stats)

				If Not Thisform.poDataMgr.Update([crSigPrNfe])
					=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Update - crSigPrNfe)])
					llOks = .F.
				Endif
			Endif
		EndIf 		
		llNfe = .T.
	Endif
Endif

If llOks
	If (Thisform.poDataMgr.Commit() < 1)
		=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (Commit)])
		llOks = .F.
	EndIf
EndIf

If Used([crNotas])
	Select crNotas
	Scan
		If Not crNotas.OKs
			=Messagebox([Verifique os Erros Na Operaçăo "] + Alltrim(crNotas.Emps) + [-] + Alltrim(crNotas.Dopes) + ;
				[-] + Alltrim(Str(crNotas.Numes, 6)) + [":] + Chr(13) + ;
				crNotas.Erros, 0+64, [Checagem de Erros])
		Endif
	Endscan
EndIf 
If llOks
	If Not llNfe	&& so mostra mensagem se năo entrou no processo da NFe
		=Messagebox([Arquivos Gerados Corretamente!!!], 0+48, [Geraçăo de Arquivo])
	Endif
Else
	=Messagebox([Nenhum Registro de Nota Foi Processado. Reprocesse!!!], 0+16, [Geraçăo de Arquivo])
	Thisform.poDataMgr.Rollback()
Endif

Thisform.LimpaSelecao()

Thisform.cmdSelecionar.Click(.T.)

Return .T.
* Fim ********************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE geranfeinutilizadas
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE geranfeinutilizadas
parameters pEmp, pSerie, pCnpj, pNFi, pNFf

Public cId, cCnpj, cDEmis, cEmail, cConteudoTXT, cConteudoXML, cConteudoPDF, cPathUni, cLote, cRecibo, cProt
Public lcPEnvio, lcPEnviado, lcPEnvioEmLote, lcPErro, lcPRetorno, lcPValidar, lcPBKenviados, lcPEmProc, ;
	lcPAssinado, lcPValidado, lcPAutorizados, lcPPdf, lcPBkp, lcChr, lcTpImp, lcPTxt
Public lcPathNFe, lcDanfe, lcUniNFe, lcLog, lcBKP, lcCnpj

Private cPathO, lcArq, llOK, lcQuery, lnIni, cPath, lcTxtAlt
Private lnQtdArq, laTxts, llRet, lcDest, lcConf,llScan, lnEmi

llRet=.T.
llScan = .F.			&& Seta que năo está sendo usado o serviço SCAN

* pega configuracoes de nfe e informacoes do cadastro da empresa
lcEmp = Padr(pEmp, 3)	&& empresa

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdEmp Where CEmps = '] + pEmp + [']
If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalEmp]) < 1)
	=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalEmp)])
	llRet=.F.
Endif

cPathUni = Alltrim(LocalEmp.pastas)

lcChr = Chr(13) + Chr(10)
lcPEnvio = "envio\"
lcPEnviado = "Enviado\"
lcPEnvioEmLote = "EnvioEmLote\"
lcPEmProc = "Enviado\EmProcessamento\"
lcPErro= "Erro\"
lcPRetorno="Retorno\"
lcPValidar="Validar\"
lcPBKenviados="BKenviados\"
lcPAssinado="Assinado\"
lcPValidado="Validado\"
lcPAutorizados = "Enviado\Autorizados\"
lcPDenegados = "Enviado\Denegados\"
lcPPdf = "PDF\"
lcPBkp = Alltrim(LocalParac.direxpsdfs)
lcPBkp = Iif(!Empty(lcPBkp),lcPBkp,cPathUni+'BKP\')
lcPTXTALT = "TXTALT\"

Set Deleted On
Set Date To brit
Set Century On
Set Exact On

lcSer = Alltrim(pSerie)
lcSer = Iif(Val(lcSer)=0, [001], Transform(Val(lcSer), "@L, 999"))

lcCnpj= Alltrim(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(LocalEmp.Cgcs, [.], []), [-], []), [/], []))
lcPathNFe= cPathUni + lcCnpj + "\"

** Mena 15/01/2024 - pasta txt do uninfe acrescida do cnpj para năo misturar informaçőes
lcPTxt = "TXT\" + lcCnpj + "\"
lcTxtpath = cPathUni + lcPTxt
If Not Directory(lcTxtpath)
	Mkdir &lcTxtpath
Endif

lcLog  = cPathUni + lcPTxt + 'logNfe.txt'

If Empty(cPathUni)
	=Strtofile(Ttoc(Datetime())+[-Path năo configurado no sistema.], lcLog, .T.)
	llRet=.F.		&& nao entra no processo NFe se o path nao estiver configurado
Endif

lcMsg = ''

**** Verifica se a conexao com a internet está ativa ****
*!*	IF not thisform.conectado()
*!*		lcMsg = [Nao ha conexao com a internet.. Verifique!!!]
*!*		llRet=.F.		&& nao entra no processo NFe se o path nao estiver configurado
*!*	ENDIF

Do While llRet
	
	**** prepara pastas para controle do envio de XMLs ****
	lcDanfe  = cPathUni + "unidanfe.exe"
	lcUniNFe = cPathUni + "uninfe.exe"
	cPath = cPathUni + lcPTxt 
	&&	SET DEFAULT TO &cPath
	Delete File cPath+[*.XML]

	lnAca = Thisform.cntOperacoes.optAcao.Value

	**** testa se já existe uma instancia do uninfe rodando - cria arquivo vazio no envio e verifica se foi lido****
	lcConf = lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+'uninfe-alt-con.xml'
	=Strtofile([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?><altConfUniNFe></altConfUniNFe>], lcConf, .T.)
	=Thisform.esperauniler(lcConf, 5)
	If File(lcConf) 	&&Ativa UniNFe para controle das NFEs
		cComando = lcUniNFe
		Run /N &cComando
	Endif

	If lnAca = 4		&& inutilizaçăo de numeracao
		=Strtofile(lcChr+Ttoc(Datetime())+[-]+[Inulilizaçăo de numeraçăo], lcLog, .T.)	&& grava cabecalho da nota no log
		Thisform.InuNfe(pSerie, pNFi, pNFf)
	Endif

	If lnAca = 7		&& inutilizaçăo de numeracao de NFCe
		=Strtofile(lcChr+Ttoc(Datetime())+[-]+[Inulilizaçăo de numeraçăo], lcLog, .T.)	&& grava cabecalho da nota no log
		Thisform.InuNfCe(pSerie, pNFi, pNFf)
	Endif

*!*		If lnQtdArq > 0

*!*			lcTxt = laTxts[1,1]
*!*			lcArq=Thisform.conver2Xml(lcTxt, cPath)

*!*			**** prepara pastas para controle do envio de XMLs ****
*!*			lcBKP = lcPBkp+cCnpj+[\]+Substr(cDEmis, 1, 6)+[\]	&& seta pasta de buckup
*!*			If Not Directory(lcBKP)
*!*				Mkdir &lcBKP
*!*			Endif
*!*			**** limpa pasta - exclui arquivos de retorno ****
*!*			Delete File lcPathNFe + lcPRetorno + [*-nfe-ret.xml]
*!*			Delete File lcPathNFe + lcPRetorno + [*-pro-rec.xml]
*!*			Delete File lcPathNFe + lcPRetorno + [*.err]
*!*			Delete File lcPathNFe + lcPRetorno + [*-sit.XML]

*!*			=Strtofile(lcChr+Ttoc(Datetime())+[-]+cId, lcLog, .T.)	&& grava cabecalho da nota no log

*!*			Do Case
*!*			Case lnAca = 1		&&emissao
*!*				Do Case
*!*				Case Inlist(crNotas.stats, '   ', 'PEN')
*!*					lnEmi = Thisform.EmiteNFe(lcArq)
*!*					If lnEmi = 1
*!*						Replace stats With 'EMI' In crNotas
*!*						Replace statts With '0' In crNotas
*!*					Endif
*!*					If lnEmi = 2
*!*						Replace stats With 'DEN' In crNotas
*!*						Replace statts With '0' In crNotas
*!*					Endif
*!*					If lnEmi = 0
*!*						If Inlist(crNotas.statts, '3', '4')	&& esta aguardando recibo ou protocolo
*!*							Replace stats With 'PEN' In crNotas
*!*						Endif
*!*					Endif
*!*					Replace ids With cId In crNotas
*!*					Replace lotes With cLote In crNotas
*!*					Replace recibos With cRecibo In crNotas
*!*					Replace prots With cProt In crNotas
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'EMI'
*!*					lcMsg='NF já emitida'
*!*					Messagebox(lcMsg, 0+64, [Emissăo de NFe])
*!*					Thisform.EmiteNFe(lcArq)			&& imprime o DANFE
*!*					lcMsg=''
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'CAN'
*!*					lcMsg='NF cancelada, năo pode ser emitida'
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'DEN'
*!*					lcMsg='NF denegada, năo pode ser emitida'
*!*				Endcase
*!*			Case lnAca = 2		&&cancelamento
*!*				Do Case
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = '   '
*!*					lcMsg='Esta NF năo pode ser cancelada pois ainda năo foi emitida'
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'EMI'
*!*					If Thisform.canNFe()
*!*						Replace crNotas.stats With 'CAN'
*!*						Replace crNotas.prots With cProt
*!*					Endif
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'CAN'
*!*					lcMsg='NF já cancelada.'
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'DEN'
*!*					lcMsg='NF denegada.'
*!*				Case crNotas.stats = 'PEN'
*!*					If Thisform.consnfe()
*!*						Thisform.EmiteNFe('PEN')
*!*					Endif
*!*					Thisform.canNFe()
*!*				Endcase
*!*			Case lnAca = 3		&&consulta
*!*				If Thisform.consnfe()
*!*					Thisform.EmiteNFe('PEN')
*!*				Endif
*!*			Case lnAca = 5		&&visualizacao
*!*				Do Case
*!*				Case Inlist(crNotas.stats, '   ', 'PEN')
*!*					=Thisform.EmiteNFe(lcArq, 5)
*!*				Otherwise
*!*					Messagebox('Visualiza somente NFe năo enviada', 0+64, [Visualizaçăo do DANFE])
*!*				Endcase
*!*			Otherwise
*!*			Endcase
*!*			lcOrig=cPath+lcTxt
*!*			Delete File &lcOrig
*!*		Else
*!*			lcMsg=Iif(!Inlist(lnAca,4,6,7), 'Năo houve seleçăo de notas.', '')	&& se năo é inutilizaçăo tem que ter nota selecionada
*!*		Endif

	***** Se UNINFE setado para SCAN, voltar para SEFAZ *****
	If llScan
		lcConf = cPathUni+lcPTxt+'uninfe-alt-con.xml'
		=Strtofile([], lcConf)
		=Strtofile([<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>], lcConf, .T.)
		=Strtofile([<altConfUniNFe>], lcConf, .T.)
		=Strtofile([<tpEmis>1</tpEmis>], lcConf, .T.)
		=Strtofile([</altConfUniNFe>], lcConf, .T.)

		lcDest=lcPathNFe+lcPEnvio+'uninfe-alt-con.xml'
		=Strtofile(lcChr+Ttoc(Datetime())+[-Muda configuraçăo do UniNFe para SEFAZ], lcLog, .T.)	&& grava cabecalho da requisicao no log
		Copy File &lcConf To &lcDest
		llScan = .F.			&& Seta que está sendo usado o serviço SCAN
	Endif

	Exit
Enddo

If !Empty(lcMsg)
	Messagebox(lcMsg, 0+64, [Emissăo de NFe])
Endif


Release cId, cCnpj, cDEmis, cEmail, cConteudoTXT, cConteudoXML, cConteudoPDF, cPathUni, cLote, cRecibo, cProt
Release lcPEnvio, lcPEnviado, lcPEnvioEmLote, lcPErro, lcPRetorno, lcPValidar, lcPBKenviados, ;
	lcPAssinado, lcPValidado, lcPAutorizados, lcPPdf, lcPBkp, lcChr, lcTpImp, lcPTxt
Release lcPathNFe, lcDanfe, lcUniNFe, lcLog, lcBKP, lcCnpj

Return llRet

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE impdsimpl
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE impdsimpl
	set step on
	lcQ = [Select * from sigmvnfi Where empdopnums = '] + csOperacoes.emps + csOperacoes.dopes + PADL(alltrim(STR(csOperacoes.numes)),6) + [']
	If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQ, [crNf]) < 1)
		=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crNf)])
		Return 0
	Endif

	lcXml = crNf.Nfexml
	lcInfprot = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<infProt","</infProt>",1)
	nProt = STREXTRACT(lcInfprot ,"<nProt>","</nProt>",1)
	nDatarec = STREXTRACT(lcInfprot ,"<dhRecbto>","</dhRecbto>",1)
	lcProt = nProt + " " + SUBSTR(nDatarec, 9, 2) + "/" + SUBSTR(nDatarec, 6, 2) + "/" + SUBSTR(nDatarec, 1, 4) + " " + SUBSTR(nDatarec, 12, 8) 
	lcChave = STREXTRACT(lcInfprot ,"<chNFe>","</chNFe>",1)
	lcChaveA = "Chave de acesso"
	lcProtA = "Protocolo de autorizacao de uso"
	lcDanfeS = "DANFE SIMPLIFICADO"
	lcFin = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<finNFe>","</finNFe>",1)
	lcFin = IIF(lcFin=="1", "1 - Saida", "0 - Entrada")
	lcNota = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<nNF>","</nNF>",1)
	lcSerie = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<serie>","</serie>",1)
	lcNumero = "Numero " + PADL(alltrim(lcNota),6,"0") + "/Serie " + lcSerie
	lcEmissao = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<dhEmi>","</dhEmi>",1)
	lcEmissao = "Emissao " + SUBSTR(lcEmissao, 9, 2) + "/" + SUBSTR(lcEmissao, 6, 2) + "/" + SUBSTR(lcEmissao, 1, 4) 
	lcEmit = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<emit>","</emit>",1)
	xNomee = STREXTRACT(lcEmit,"<xNome>","</xNome>",1)
	xCnpje = STREXTRACT(lcEmit,"<CNPJ>","</CNPJ>",1)
	xIEe = STREXTRACT(lcEmit,"<IE>","</IE>",1)
	xUFe = STREXTRACT(lcEmit,"<UF>","</UF>",1)
	lcLinha1e = "REMETENTE: " + xNomee
	lcLinha2e = "CNPJ: " + xCnpje + " INSCR. ESTATUAL: " + xIEe + "  UF: " + xUFe
	lcDest = STREXTRACT(lcXml,"<dest>","</dest>",1) 
	xNomed = STREXTRACT(lcDest,"<xNome>","</xNome>",1)
	xCnpjd = STREXTRACT(lcDest,"<CNPJ>","</CNPJ>",1)
	xCpfd = STREXTRACT(lcDest,"<CPF>","</CPF>",1)
	xIEd = STREXTRACT(lcDest,"<IE>","</IE>",1)
	xUFd = STREXTRACT(lcDest,"<UF>","</UF>",1)
	lcLinha1d = "DESTINATARIO: " + xNomed
	if !EMPTY(xCnpjd)
		lcLinha2d = "CNPJ: " + xCnpjd + " INSCR. ESTATUAL: " + xIEd + "  UF: " + xUFd
	ELSE
		lcLinha2d = "CPF:  " + xCpfd + "  UF: " + xUFd
	ENDIF

	Create Cursor csDsimpl (fin c(30), numero c(30), ;
						   emissao c(30), chavea c(30), chave c(50), ;
						   linha1e c(70), linha2e c(70), linha1d c(70), linha2d c(70), danfes c(30), prot c(60), prota c(60))
	insert into csDsimpl (fin, numero, emissao, chavea, chave, linha1e, linha2e, linha1d, linha2d, danfes, prot, prota) ;
		   values(lcFin, lcNumero, lcEmissao, lcChaveA, lcChave, lcLinha1e, lcLinha2e, lcLinha1d, ;
		   linha2d, lcDanfes, lcProt, lcProta)
	
	select csDsimpl 
	Report form SigreDsi Preview NoConsole		

		
											   

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Release
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Release
ThisForm.poDataMgr.Release

=DoDefault()
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
parameters pcMov, pcSerie, pOperas

Thisform.pMovimentacao = Iif(Type([pcMov])=[C],pcMov,[])

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = ThisForm.Caption
ThisForm.cntSombra.lblTitulo.Caption = ThisForm.Caption

With ThisForm
	.poDataMgr = CreateObject([fSqlConector], .Name)

	If (.poDataMgr.pnIdconn > 0)
		With .poDataMgr
			.AddCursor([SigPrNfe], [cIdChaves], [crSigPrNfe])
			.AddCursor([SigMvNfi], [cIdChaves], [crSigMvNfi])
		EndWith

		.Versao = [2.0.4]

		.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Enabled 	    = .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getSeries.Enabled 	= .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getArquivos.Enabled 	= .f.
		.cntOperacoes.optProcessados.Option1.Enabled = .t.
		.cntOperacoes.optProcessados.Option2.Enabled = .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getDtIni.Enabled 		= .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getDtFin.Enabled 		= .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getInuIni.Enabled 	= .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getInuFim.Enabled 	= .t.
		.cmdSelecionar.Enabled = .t.
		.cntOperacoes.getDtIni.Value		= Date()
		.cntOperacoes.getDtFin.Value 		= Date()
		.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Value			= _Empr
		.cntOperacoes.cmbRegime.Value 		= [Simples Nacional]
		.cntOperacoes.cmbRegime.Enabled     = .t.
		.cmdBtnGrade.btnMarcaTudo.Enabled   = .f.
		.cmdBtnGrade.btnDesmarcar.Enabled   = .f.
		.cmdBtnGrade.btnDocumentos.Enabled  = .f.
		.cmdBtnForm.btnLimpar.Enabled       = .f.
		.cmdBtnForm.btnCopiar.Enabled       = .f.

		lcOnE = On([Error])
		On Error lnOnE = Error()
		lnOnE = 0
		Declare Integer ConsisteInscricaoEstadual In [DllInscE32.Dll] String @Insc, String @Uf
		.ValidaIE = (lnOnE = 0)
		On Error &lcOnE.

		.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPam], [LocalParam], .f., .f., [TpInstalas, Grpurifics])
		If Not Used([LocalParam])
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CursorQuery - LocalParam)])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select LocalParam
		Go Top In LocalParam
		.Versaol = [4.00]	&& mena - 24/11/2017	- seta a versao do layout do xml

		.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPac], [LocalParac], .f., .f., [DirRps, PafEcfs, direxpsdfs, nfhverao, cifcnpjs, cifconts, cifendes, ciftels])
		If Not Used([LocalParac])
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CursorQuery - LocalParac)])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select LocalParac
		Go Top In LocalParac
		
		ThisForm.cntOperacoes.chkHVerao.Value = LocalParac.nfhverao
		ThisForm.cntOperacoes.chkHVerao.Refresh 
		If Not .ChecarDirs()
			Return .f.		
		EndIf

		=DoDefault()

		With .cntGrade.grdOperacoes
			.ColumnCount  	   = 9
			.RecordSource 	   = [csOperacoes]
			.HeaderHeight 	   = 19
			.DeleteMark   	   = .f.
			.RecordMark   	   = .f.
			.ReadOnly     	   = .f.
			.Scrollbars   	   =  2
			.AllowHeaderSizing = .f.
			.AllowRowSizing    = .f.

			.Column1.ControlSource = [csOperacoes.SelImp]
			.Column1.Movable   = .f.
			.Column1.Resizable = .f.
			.Column1.ReadOnly  = .f.
			.Column1.Sparse    = .f.
			.Column1.Check1.AutoSize = .t.

			.Column2.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Numes]
			.Column3.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Datas]
			.Column4.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Valos]
			.Column5.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Notas]
			.Column6.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Series]
			.Column7.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Dopes]
			.Column8.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.Emps]
			.Column9.ControlSource  = [csOperacoes.stats]
			
			For I=2 To .ColumnCount
				lcCol = Alltrim(Str(I))
				.Column&lcCol..FontName = [Courier New]
				.Column&lcCol..Movable   = .f.
				.Column&lcCol..Resizable = .f.
				.Column&lcCol..ReadOnly  = .t.
			Next
		EndWith

		lcQuery = [Select Cods From SigCdSer Where ImpNfs = 3 Order By Cods]
		If (.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalSer]) < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalSer)])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Go Top In LocalSer
		If Not Eof([LocalSer])
			.cntOperacoes.getSeries.Value = IIF(TYPE('pcSerie') = "C", PADR(alltrim(pcSerie),3), LocalSer.Cods)
			.cntOperacoes.getDtIni.SetFocus
		Else
			.cntOperacoes.getSeries.SetFocus
		EndIf
		
		If Type([pOperas])=[C] 
			ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optTipos.Value = Iif(pOperas=[E],2,1)
		EndIf 
		
	Else
		=Messagebox([Impossível Efetuar Conexăo Com o Servidor de Banco de Dados...], 0+48, [CreateObject])
		Return .f.
	ENDIF
	thisform.cntOperacoes.versao.Caption = [Versao :]+thisform.versaol
	
	If Not Empty(ThisForm.pMovimentacao)
		=Thisform.Podatamgr.CursorQuery([SigMvNfi],[crAutNfi],[EmpDopNums],ThisForm.pMovimentacao)
		Thisform.cntOperacoes.getDtIni.Value = crAutNfi.Emis
		Thisform.cntOperacoes.getDtFin.Value = crAutNfi.Emis
		Thisform.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Value	 = crAutNfi.Emps
		ThisForm.Selecionar()
	EndIf 
	
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Load
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Load
=fConfigGeral()

Create Cursor csOperacoes (SelImp l(1), Emps c(3), Dopes c(20), Numes n(6), Datas d(8), Valos n(12,2), ;
						   Notas c(10), Series c(3), NFMemo m(4), Erros m(4), Tipos n(1), stats c(3), ids c(47), lotes c(15), recibos c(15), prots c(15), statts c(1))
Index On Notas + Emps + Dopes + Str(Numes, 6) Tag Notas

=DoDefault()
* Fim ********************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.cmdBtnForm
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 7
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If (This.Value = 2) && Se Clicou em Copiar Faz a Checagem
	Select SelImp, Count(1) as Selecionados ;
	  From csOperacoes ;
	 Where SelImp ;
	 Group By SelImp ;
	  Into Cursor csSeles
	  
	If (csSeles.Selecionados < 1) and (INLIST(this.Parent.cntOperacoes.optAcao.Value,1,2,3,5))   
		=Messagebox([Nenhum Lançamento Foi Encontrado!!!], 0+48, [Atençăo!!!])
		ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getSeries.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf
EndIf 

Do Case
	Case (This.Value = 1) And This.btnLimpar.Enabled
		 * Limpar Seleçăo
		 ThisForm.LimpaSelecao()
		 
	Case (This.Value = 2) And This.btnCopiar.Enabled
		 * Processar
		 ThisForm.Processamento()
		 
	Case This.Value = 3
		 * Sair
		 ThisForm.Release
EndCase
* Fim ********************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE btnSair.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE btnSair.Click
ThisForm.Release
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.cntGrade.GrdOperacoes.Column1.Check1
* Classe: checkbox (Base: checkbox)
* Registro: 11
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
NoDefault
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE MouseDown
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE MouseDown
LParameters nButton, nShift, nXCoord, nYCoord

Local SelImp

m.SelImp = (Not csOperacoes.SelImp)

Select csOperacoes
Gather Memvar Fields SelImp
ThisForm.cntGrade.GrdOperacoes.Refresh

NoDefault
* Fim ********************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE MouseUp
------------------------------------------------------------

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE KeyPress
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE KeyPress
LParameters nKeyCode, nShiftAltCtrl

Local SelImp

If InList(nKeyCode, 13, 32)
	m.SelImp = (Not csOperacoes.SelImp)

	Select csOperacoes
	Gather Memvar Fields SelImp
	ThisForm.cntGrade.GrdOperacoes.Refresh

	NoDefault
EndIf
* Fim ********************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.cntOperacoes.getSeries
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 35

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista

If Not Empty(This.Value)
	Declare laFil[1,2]
	laFil[1,1] = [ImpNfs]
	laFil[1,2] = 3

	loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaExt], ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn, [SigCdSer], ;
						   [crListaRemota], [Cods], This.Value, [Seleçăo], .t., [ImpNfs], @laFil)

	If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro
		loLista.mAddColuna([Cods],  [], [Série])
		loLista.mAddColuna([Descs], [], [Descriçăo])
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	This.Value = crListaRemota.Cods
	Use In crListaRemota
EndIf
This.Refresh
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.cntOperacoes.cmdInu
* Classe: commandbutton (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 61
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
ThisForm.CntInu.GrdInu.RecordSource = ''
If Used('nfAinu')

	lcEmp = ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Value
	
	Select 1 as nMarca, * From nfAinu where Emps = lcEmp Into Cursor csInutil ReadWrite
	Select csInutil
	GO top
	With ThisForm.CntInu.GrdInu
		.RecordSource = 'csInutil'
		.Column1.ControlSource = 'csInutil.Emps'
		.Column2.ControlSource = 'csInutil.Series'
		.Column3.ControlSource = 'csInutil.Notai'
		.Column4.ControlSource = 'csInutil.Notaf'
		.Column5.ControlSource = 'csInutil.Cnpj'
		.Column6.ControlSource = 'csInutil.nMarca'
		.Refresh
	Endwith
EndIf

ThisForm.CntInu.Visible = .T.
ENDPROC

* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.Commandgroup1
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 65
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE btnInu.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE btnInu.Click
	lcQuery= [select distinct emps, substring(ids,7,14) as cnpj, substring(ids,23,3) as series, substring(ids,26,9) as notai, substring(ids,26,9) as notaf from sigprnfe where stats = 'xxx' ] 
	If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [nfAInu]) < 1)
		=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (nfAInu)])
		Return 0
	Endif

*!*		lcQuery= [select distinct emps, substring(ids,7,14) as cnpj, substring(ids,23,3) as series, substring(ids,26,9) as notai, substring(ids,26,9) as notaf from sigprnfe where stats = 'EMI' ] +; 
*!*		[union ] +;
*!*		[(select emps, substring(ids,5,14) as cnpj, substring(ids,21,3) as series, substring(ids,24,9) as notai, substring(ids,33,9) as notaf from sigprnfe where stats = 'INU')]

	lcQuery= [select distinct case when substring(ids,7,14) = '12136108000195' then 'SVP' else emps end as emps, ] + ;
			[substring(ids,7,14) as cnpj, substring(ids,23,3) as series, substring(ids,26,9) as notai, substring(ids,26,9) as notaf ] + ;
			[from sigprnfe where stats = 'EMI' and substring(ids,26,9) <> '' ] + ;
			[union ] + ;
			[select distinct case when substring(ids,5,14) = '12136108000195' then 'SVP' else emps end as emps, ] + ;
			[substring(ids,5,14) as cnpj, substring(ids,21,3) as series, substring(ids,24,9) as notai, substring(ids,33,9) as notaf ] + ;
			[from sigprnfe where stats = 'INU' and substring(ids,24,9) <> '' ] + ; 
			[order by 1,2,4,5 ]
			
	If (Thisform.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [nfUsadas]) < 1)
		=Messagebox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (nfUsadas)])
		Return 0
	Endif
	
	SELECT * from nfUsadas where cnpj != '              ' order by cnpj, series, notai into cursor nfUsadas1
	
	lcNotaInu = 1
	SELECT nfUsadas1
	GO top
	lcCnpj = nfUsadas1.cnpj 	
	lcSeries = nfUsadas1.series 	

	do while !EOF()
		do while nfUsadas1.cnpj = lcCnpj and nfUsadas1.series = lcSeries
			if lcNotaInu < VAL(nfUsadas1.notai)
				SELECT nfAinu
				APPEND BLANK
				replace notai with PADL(ALLTRIM(STR(lcNotaInu)),8,'0')
			ENDIF
			do while lcNotaInu < VAL(nfUsadas1.notai)
				replace emps with nfUsadas1.emps
				replace cnpj with nfUsadas1.cnpj
				replace series with nfUsadas1.series
				replace notaf with PADL(ALLTRIM(STR(lcNotaInu)),8,'0')
				lcNotaInu = lcNotaInu + 1
			ENDdo
			lcNotaInu = VAL(nfUsadas1.notaf)+1
			exit
		ENDDO
		
		if nfUsadas1.cnpj != lcCnpj or nfUsadas1.series != lcSeries
			SELECT nfUsadas1
			lcCnpj = nfUsadas1.cnpj 	
			lcSeries = nfUsadas1.series 	
			lcNotaInu = 1
			loop
		endif
		SELECT nfUsadas1
		SKIP
	ENDDO
	
	
SELECT nfAinu
GO top
BROWSE
SELECT nfAinu
GO top

EXPORT TO .\inutiliza xl5 
MESSAGEBOX('Lista gravada no arquivo inutiliza.xls')




ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.CntInu.cmdProc
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 84
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If Not InList(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.optAcao.Value,4,7)
	Return 0
EndIf 

If Empty(ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Value)
	MessageBox([Empresa năo Informada.],0+48,[Aviso])
	Return 0
EndIf 

lcEmp = ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getEmps.Value 

Select csInutil
Go Top
Select Count(1) as Selecionados From csInutil Into Cursor csSelesInu
	  
If (csSelesInu.Selecionados < 1)
	=Messagebox([Nenhum Lançamento Foi Encontrado!!!], 0+48, [Atençăo!!!])
	ThisForm.cntOperacoes.getSeries.SetFocus
	Return 0
EndIf

ThisForm.SelecionarInutilizadas()

Select csInutil 
Go Top
Scan 
	If csInutil.nMarca <> 1
		Loop 
	EndIf 
	ThisForm.ProcessamentoInutilizadas(csInutil.Emps, csInutil.Series, csInutil.Cnpj, csInutil.Notai, csInutil.Notaf)
	Select csInutil
EndScan 

ThisForm.CntInu.LostFocus()

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGPRNFE.cmdBtnGrade
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 85
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Do Case
   Case (This.Value = 1) And This.btnMarcaTudo.Enabled
		* Marca Tudo
		Select csOperacoes
		Replace All SelImp With .t.
		Go Top
		ThisForm.cntGrade.GrdOperacoes.Refresh
		 
   Case (This.Value = 2) And This.btnDesmarcar.Enabled
   		* Desmarcar
		Select csOperacoes
		Replace All SelImp With .f.
		Go Top
		ThisForm.cntGrade.GrdOperacoes.Refresh
		 
   Case (This.Value = 3) And This.btnDocumentos.Enabled
   		* Operaçőes
		Do Form SigMvExp With csOperacoes.Dopes, [C], csOperacoes.Numes, csOperacoes.Emps, .t.

   Case (This.Value = 4) And This.btnDSimpl.Enabled
		Thisform.ImpDSimpl()
EndCase
* Fim ********************************************************************************************
ENDPROC
